========
1. 1. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.
2. 2. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
3. 3. Line base and side with baking parchment.
4. 4. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 5. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 6. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 7. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 8. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 9. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
10. 10. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
11. 11. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 12. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 13. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 14. Serve warm.

10. 8. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
4. 9. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 10. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 11. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 12. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 13. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 14. Repeat remaining flour and milk.

10. 14. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
must step 1 happen before step 13?
========
1. 1. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.
4. 2. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 3. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 4. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 5. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 6. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 7. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
3. 8. Line base and side with baking parchment.
11. 9. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 10. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 11. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 12. Serve warm.

5. 4. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 5. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 6. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 7. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 8. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
11. 9. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 10. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 11. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 12. Serve warm.
2. 13. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
3. 14. Line base and side with baking parchment.

5. 9. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 10. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 11. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 12. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 13. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
2. 14. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
must step 1 happen before step 14?
========

11. 2. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 3. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 4. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 5. Serve warm.

========
2. 1. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
3. 2. Line base and side with baking parchment.
1. 3. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.
10. 4. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
11. 5. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 6. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 7. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 8. Serve warm.
4. 9. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 10. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 11. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 12. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 13. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 14. Repeat remaining flour and milk.

3. 8. Line base and side with baking parchment.
10. 9. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
1. 10. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.
11. 11. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 12. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 13. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 14. Serve warm.

must step 1 happen before step 9?
========
2. 1. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
10. 2. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
4. 3. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 4. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 5. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 6. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 7. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 8. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
3. 9. Line base and side with baking parchment.

12. 12. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 13. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 14. Serve warm.

14. 5. Serve warm.
10. 6. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
1. 7. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.
4. 8. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 9. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 10. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 11. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 12. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 13. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
3. 14. Line base and side with baking parchment.

11. 11. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 12. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 13. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 14. Serve warm.
must step 2 happen before step 3?
========
3. 1. Line base and side with baking parchment.
2. 2. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
1. 3. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.
4. 4. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 5. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 6. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 7. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 8. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 9. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
11. 10. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 11. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 12. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 13. Serve warm.

4. 2. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 3. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 4. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 5. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 6. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 7. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
2. 8. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
1. 9. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.
10. 10. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
11. 11. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 12. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 13. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 14. Serve warm.
must step 8 happen before step 9?
========

4. 8. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 9. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 10. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 11. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 12. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 13. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
1. 14. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.
must step 3 happen before step 14?
========

7. 6. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 7. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 8. Repeat remaining flour and milk.

2. 14. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
must step 13 happen before step 14?
========
3. 1. Line base and side with baking parchment.
11. 2. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 3. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 4. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 5. Serve warm.
4. 6. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 7. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 8. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 9. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 10. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 11. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
10. 12. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.

8. 5. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 6. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
1. 7. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.
11. 8. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 9. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 10. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 11. Serve warm.
10. 12. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
2. 13. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
3. 14. Line base and side with baking parchment.
must step 7 happen before step 13?
========

7. 4. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 5. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.

13. 12. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 13. Serve warm.
2. 14. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
must step 8 happen before step 14?
========
4. 1. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 2. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 3. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 4. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 5. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 6. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
3. 7. Line base and side with baking parchment.

5. 2. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 3. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 4. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 5. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 6. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
10. 7. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
2. 8. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
3. 9. Line base and side with baking parchment.
11. 10. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 11. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 12. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 13. Serve warm.
1. 14. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.
must step 8 happen before step 14?

13. 9. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 10. Serve warm.
3. 11. Line base and side with baking parchment.
2. 12. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
1. 13. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.
10. 14. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
must step 12 happen before step 13?
========
4. 1. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 2. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 3. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 4. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 5. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 6. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
11. 7. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 8. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 9. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 10. Serve warm.

6. 11. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 12. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 13. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.

12. 6. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 7. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 8. Serve warm.
4. 9. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 10. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 11. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 12. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 13. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 14. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
must step 3 happen before step 4?
========
10. 1. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
3. 2. Line base and side with baking parchment.
1. 3. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.
4. 4. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 5. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 6. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 7. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 8. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 9. Repeat remaining flour and milk.

12. 12. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 13. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 14. Serve warm.
must step 8 happen before step 9?
========
10. 1. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
4. 2. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 3. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 4. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 5. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 6. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 7. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
2. 8. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
1. 9. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.

12. 3. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 4. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 5. Serve warm.
3. 6. Line base and side with baking parchment.
1. 7. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.
2. 8. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
4. 9. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 10. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 11. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 12. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 13. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 14. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
must step 7 happen before step 8?
========

6. 8. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 9. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 10. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 11. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
10. 12. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
3. 13. Line base and side with baking parchment.
2. 14. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
must step 5 happen before step 14?
========
11. 1. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 2. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 3. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 4. Serve warm.

3. 14. Line base and side with baking parchment.
must step 5 happen before step 13?
========
11. 1. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 2. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 3. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 4. Serve warm.
2. 5. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
10. 6. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
4. 7. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 8. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 9. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 10. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 11. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 12. Repeat remaining flour and milk.

4. 5. Beat butter , caster sugar and vanilla in a bowl for 8 mins or till pale and creamy ( by hand or electric beater ).
5. 6. Add the eggs , 1 at a time , beating well after each addition.
6. 7. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 8. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 9. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 10. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
1. 11. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.
10. 12. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
2. 13. Brush around 22cm ( base measurement ) cake tin with melted butter to grease.
3. 14. Line base and side with baking parchment.

========

6. 10. Stir in ground almonds.
7. 11. Add half the flour and half the milk.
8. 12. Use a wooden spoon to stir until well combined.
9. 13. Repeat remaining flour and milk.
1. 14. Preheat the oven to 170 C / Gas mark 3.
must step 6 happen before step 14?
========
11. 1. Spoon mixture into the tin and smooth the surface.
12. 2. Bake in the oven for 30-35 mins or until a skewer inserted into the centre comes out clean.
13. 3. Set aside in the pan for 10 mins to cool slightly before turning onto a serving plate.
14. 4. Serve warm.
10. 5. Arrange the apple , slightly overlapping , over the base of the prepared tin.
